results, let me know - most players now get them as emailed PDF reports as standard.<L.31.1>

<Z>Other Games <C> If you aren't aware, I can generally sort out a second (or more) team in a game - I run more than one game of<L.31.1>
Gameplan Baseball, Hoopplan, Slapshot, Raceplan, Run Chase and Gameplan on a fortnightly basis (so I could alternate games on<L.31.1>
different weeks) as well as Gridstats (NFL), Soccer Stats (Premier League) and Play On (AFL Aussie Rules) during their seasons on<L.31.1>
a weekly basis. If you fancy a new, or better, additional challenge, let me know and I can provide details.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Email Results <C> If you think results are late, please make sure you wait until Monday before chasing up results, and <L.31.1>
before you do check out the Latest News at www.pbmsports.com - if I am running late I'll post a notice there.<L.31.1>
